## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics (continuous-time growth models)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt is the time-derivative of population size P, indicating an ODE-based population growth model. Common structures encode density-independent growth, density dependence (carrying capacity), Allee effects at low P, time-varying environments, and external removals/harvesting as functions of t and P.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Malthusian (exponential) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent per-capita growth)
- Exponential with background immigration: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (population grows plus constant influx)
- Linear density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 (self-limitation leading to saturation)
- Logistic (Verhulst) differential form: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (carrying capacity via quadratic crowding)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible strength/shape of density dependence)
- Richards generalized logistic rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)**c3 (extra shape parameter for asymmetric approach to carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (per-capita growth declines logarithmically with size)
- Strong Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 * P - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (negative growth at low P, positive at intermediate P, negative near capacity)
- Weak Allee effect (smooth): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 * P) / (c2 * P + 1) (low-density suppression without hard threshold)
- Proportional harvesting/mortality: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (constant per-capita loss term)
- Constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (removal at fixed rate, risk of extinction at low P)
- Seasonally forced growth: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) * P * (1 - c4 * P) (periodic environment modulates intrinsic growth)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density independence → dP_dt proportional to P (straight-line per-capita rate dP_dt/P ≈ constant)
- Crowding/carrying capacity → negative quadratic or higher-order terms in P (sign change in dP_dt as P increases)
- Flexible saturation shape → exponent on (c * P) inside 1 - (c * P)^theta (controls whether limitation turns on early or late)
- Asymmetric approach to capacity → logarithm term log(c/P) (fast initial growth, slow late growth without a simple quadratic)
- Allee effect at low density → factors like (c * P - 1) or saturating multipliers (negative growth when P is small)
- External removals → subtraction terms independent of P (constant harvest) or proportional to P (per-capita mortality/harvest)
- Time-varying environment → coefficients that depend on t (e.g., c0 + c1*sin(c2*t) or c0 + c1*exp(-c2*(t-c3)^2))
- Regime shifts in time → smooth switching with tanh(c*(t-c0)) multiplying growth parameters (different growth rules before/after a transition)

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.17*(−1 + P/1.047)*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − exp(−0.097*P))*P
```

Let me expand this. Let me use exact coefficients:
- a = 0.1699888096710614
- b = 1.0472843670254641
- d = 10.210545156320043
- k = 0.09709294493863778

GT = a*(P/b - 1)*(1 - P/d)*P + a*(1 - P/d)*P + a*(1 - exp(-k*P))*P

Let me combine the first two terms. Factor out a*(1 - P/d)*P:
= a*(1 - P/d)*P * [(P/b - 1) + 1] + a*(1 - exp(-k*P))*P
= a*(1 - P/d)*P * (P/b) + a*(1 - exp(-k*P))*P
= a*P²/b*(1 - P/d) + a*P*(1 - exp(-k*P))
= a*P²/b - a*P³/(b*d) + a*P - a*P*exp(-k*P)

So GT = -a/(b*d) * P³ + a/b * P² + a*P - a*P*exp(-k*P)

Let me compute coefficients:
- P³ coefficient: -a/(b*d) = -0.17/(1.047*10.21) ≈ -0.01589
- P² coefficient: a/b = 0.17/1.047 ≈ 0.16225
- P coefficient: a = 0.17
- P*exp(-k*P) coefficient: -a = -0.17

So GT = c_3*P³ + c_2*P² + c_1*P + c_e*P*exp(-k*P)

where c_3 < 0, c_2 > 0, c_1 > 0, c_e < 0, k > 0.

**The GT has the form: P³*A + P²*B + P*C + P*D*exp(E*P)** where A, B, C, D, E are constants (E < 0).

This can be written as: P*(P²*A + P*B + C + D*exp(E*P))

## Candidate Analysis

= P*(P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(P*c4))
= P³*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(P*c4)

This is exactly the GT form! ✓

**Candidate 14 verdict: [MATCH]**

**Candidate 38:** P*(P²*c0+P*c1+c2) + c3 + c4*log(c5*exp(P*c6)+1)

**Candidate 71-74, 76-77:** All have exp(P*c) without P multiplier. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 73:** c0*(c1*P + c2 + c3*(P³*c4+P²*c5+c6+c7*exp(P*c8)))
